REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":9,"cache_creation_input_tokens":173,"cache_read_input_tokens":62388,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":173},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"78287838-ea77-4ec3-a486-0b6efb7b8b83","uuid":"4f7cd1f6-8db3-4de2-b16e-725a93b0d6e3"}

REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":15,"oldLines":7,"newStart":15,"newLines":10,"lines":["     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractStatus.java\"},","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/errors/ConnectExceptionMapper.java\"},","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ServerInfo.java\"},","-    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/PluginInfo.java\"}","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/PluginInfo.java\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/ConnectorHealth.java\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/ConnectorState.java\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/TaskState.java\"}","   ],","   \"symbols\": [","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/ConnectorsResource.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectorsResource\"},"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":30,"oldLines":7,"newStart":30,"newLines":10,"lines":["     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/ErrorMessage.java\", \"symbol\": \"ErrorMessage\"},","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/TaskStatus.java\", \"symbol\": \"TaskStatus\"},","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/AbstractStatus.java\", \"symbol\": \"AbstractStatus\"},","-    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectRestServer\"}","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectRestServer\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/ConnectorHealth.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectorHealth\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/ConnectorState.java\", \"symbol\": \"ConnectorState\"},","+    {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/TaskState.java\", \"symbol\": \"TaskState\"}","   ],","   \"chain\": [","     {\"repo\": \"apache/kafka\", \"path\": \"connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/ConnectRestServer.java\", \"symbol\": \"regularResources\"},"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

Version management is achieved through:\n\n1. **Plugin-level versioning**: Via query parameters in configuration endpoints\n2. **Version fields in REST responses**: ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState includes version info (filtered when undefined)\n3. **Conditional version inclusion**: Jackson's @JsonInclude with PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\n4. **Server version exposure**: Root endpoint returns server version via ServerInfo\n\nThe **public Health API** (`connect/api/health/`) represents a simplified, version-agnostic interface for external extensions, while the **REST entity classes** include internal version tracking for operational purposes.\n\nThis multi-tiered design allows:\n- Plugin versioning flexibility via query parameters\n- Stable public API contracts via the health API\n- Internal version tracking in REST responses\n- No breaking v1/v2 API versioning at the REST endpoint level\n\nThe migration from v1 to v2 (if planned) would likely involve:\n- Keeping the single REST endpoint path structure (e.g., `/connectors`)\n- Adding version fields conditionally to responses\n- Maintaining backward compatibility through JSON serialization filters\n- Evolving the public Health API without breaking external extensions"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":6,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1368,"cache_read_input_tokens":71998,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1368},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"78287838-ea77-4ec3-a486-0b6efb7b8b83","uuid":"48af4bdf-634f-4dd3-8f40-372043d87d4f"}

Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\"\n    47→}\n    48→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\\n\\n## Public Health API\\n\\nThe `connect/api/` package contains the public-facing health API definitions:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorHealth.java**: Public API class providing basic health information about a connector and its tasks. Contains name, ConnectorState, Map<Integer, TaskState>, and ConnectorType.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorState.java** (Health API): Public API class for connector health state with state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\n3. **TaskState.java** (Health API): Public API class for task health state with taskId, state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\nThese health API classes differ from the REST entity classes (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState) in that they are part of the public ConnectRestExtension API and do NOT include version fields.\\n\\n## Key Differences Between Current and Future API Versions\\n\\nThe following differences exist between the **internal REST response entities** and the **public health API**:\\n\\n**REST Response Entities** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/):\\n- Include a `version` field in TaskState and ConnectorState\\n- Use conditional JSON inclusion via @JsonInclude with NoVersionFilter\\n- Support filtering out undefined version values\\n\\n**Public Health API** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/):\\n- NO `version` field in ConnectorState or TaskState\\n- Simpler, stable API contract\\n- Used by ConnectRestExtension implementations\\n\\n## Error Response Handling\\n\\n**REST API**: Uses unified ErrorMessage class (error_code + message)\\n**Health API**: No error response class defined (not applicable for health checks)\""," }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\\n\\n## Public Health API\\n\\nThe `connect/api/` package contains the public-facing health API definitions:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorHealth.java**: Public API class providing basic health information about a connector and its tasks. Contains name, ConnectorState, Map<Integer, TaskState>, and ConnectorType.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorState.java** (Health API): Public API class for connector health state with state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\n3. **TaskState.java** (Health API): Public API class for task health state with taskId, state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\nThese health API classes differ from the REST entity classes (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState) in that they are part of the public ConnectRestExtension API and do NOT include version fields.\\n\\n## Key Differences Between Current and Future API Versions\\n\\nThe following differences exist between the **internal REST response entities** and the **public health API**:\\n\\n**REST Response Entities** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/):\\n- Include a `version` field in TaskState and ConnectorState\\n- Use conditional JSON inclusion via @JsonInclude with NoVersionFilter\\n- Support filtering out undefined version values\\n\\n**Public Health API** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/):\\n- NO `version` field in ConnectorState or TaskState\\n- Simpler, stable API contract\\n- Used by ConnectRestExtension implementations\\n\\n## Error Response Handling\\n\\n**REST API**: Uses unified ErrorMessage class (error_code + message)\\n**Health API**: No error response class defined (not applicable for health checks)\"\n    47→}\n    48→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\\n\\n## Public Health API\\n\\nThe `connect/api/` package contains the public-facing health API definitions:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorHealth.java**: Public API class providing basic health information about a connector and its tasks. Contains name, ConnectorState, Map<Integer, TaskState>, and ConnectorType.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorState.java** (Health API): Public API class for connector health state with state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\n3. **TaskState.java** (Health API): Public API class for task health state with taskId, state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\nThese health API classes differ from the REST entity classes (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState) in that they are part of the public ConnectRestExtension API and do NOT include version fields.\\n\\n## Key Differences Between Current and Future API Versions\\n\\nThe following differences exist between the **internal REST response entities** and the **public health API**:\\n\\n**REST Response Entities** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/):\\n- Include a `version` field in TaskState and ConnectorState\\n- Use conditional JSON inclusion via @JsonInclude with NoVersionFilter\\n- Support filtering out undefined version values\\n\\n**Public Health API** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/):\\n- NO `version` field in ConnectorState or TaskState\\n- Simpler, stable API contract\\n- Used by ConnectRestExtension implementations\\n\\n## Error Response Handling\\n\\n**REST API**: Uses unified ErrorMessage class (error_code + message)\\n**Health API**: No error response class defined (not applicable for health checks)\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":18,"oldLines":7,"newStart":18,"newLines":8,"lines":[" REST API implementation does not use explicit v1/v2 path-based versioning. Instead, it employs a single, stable API design with version handling implemented at the plugin configuration level.\\n\\n## Core REST API Resource Handlers\\n\\nThe main connector resource handlers are located in `connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/resources/`:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorsResource.java**: The primary REST endpoint handler for all connector operations. Provides endpoints like `/connectors`, `/connectors/{connector}`, `/connectors/{connector}/status`, and `/connectors/{connector}/tasks/{task}/status`. Implements the main connector management API without explicit version separation.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorPluginsResource.java**: Handles connector plugin discovery and configuration. Implements version handling through query parameters (e.g., `?version=latest`), using Maven's VersionRange for semantic versioning support. This is the only location where API versioning is explicitly handled.\\n\\n3. **InternalConnectResource.java**: Extends InternalClusterResource to provide internal (inter-worker) endpoints at the `/connectors` path for cluster communication. Hidden from user-facing API.\\n\\n4. **InternalClusterResource.java**: Abstract base class defining internal cluster communication endpoints like `/{connector}/tasks` (POST) and `/{connector}/fence` (PUT), used only for worker-to-worker communication.\\n\\n5. **RootResource.java**: Provides server information endpoint (`GET /`) and health check endpoint (`GET /health`).\\n\\n6. **LoggingResource.java**: Admin resource for logging level management.\\n\\n## Task Status Response Schema\\n\\nThe task status response is defined in two interconnected classes:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorStateInfo.java**: Container for connector and task state information. Contains:\\n   - `ConnectorState`: Represents connector status with state, worker_id, msg (trace), and version fields\\n   - `TaskState`: Extends AbstractState, representing individual task status with id, state, worker_id, msg, and version fields\\n   - Both use `@JsonInclude(value = JsonInclude.Include.CUSTOM, valueFilter = PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter.class)` to conditionally filter out version fields when undefined\\n\\n2. **AbstractStatus.java**: Base class defining the state enum (UNASSIGNED, RUNNING, PAUSED, FAILED, DESTROYED, RESTARTING, STOPPED) and common fields (state, trace, workerId, version, generation)\\n\\n3. **TaskStatus.java**: Runtime representation of task status, extending AbstractStatus<ConnectorTaskId>\\n\\n## Error Response Schema\\n\\n**ErrorMessage.java**: Single unified error response format with:\\n- `error_code` (int): HTTP-style error code\\n- `message` (String): Human-readable error description\\n\\nNo version-specific error responses exist. All exceptions are mapped to this format by `ConnectExceptionMapper.java`.\\n\\n## Version Routing Mechanism\\n\\n**Version handling in ConnectorPluginsResource.java**:\\n- Query parameter approach: `GET /connector-plugins/{pluginName}/config?version=<version>`\\n- Supports semantic versioning: \\\"latest\\\", \\\"1.0\\\", version ranges like \\\"[1.0,2.0)\\\"\\n- Delegates version parsing to `PluginUtils.connectorVersionRequirement(version)`\\n- Returns version-specific ConfigKeyInfo list\\n\\n**Plugin version information**:\\n- Each plugin reports its version via `PluginInfo.java`\\n- Version filtering uses Jackson's `@JsonInclude` with `NoVersionFilter` to exclude undefined versions from JSON output\\n\\n## Server Registration\\n\\n**ConnectRestServer.java**: Registers all resource classes:\\n- Regular resources: RootResource, ConnectorsResource, InternalConnectResource, ConnectorPluginsResource\\n- Admin resources: LoggingResource\\n- No separate v1/v2 resource registration chains\\n\\n## Key Finding\\n\\nThe Kafka Connect REST API uses a **single, unified API design** without explicit v1/v2 endpoint separation. Version management is achieved through:\\n1. Plugin-level versioning via query parameters in configuration endpoints\\n2. Version fields in response entities (ConnectorStateInfo, TaskState)\\n3. Conditional version field inclusion/exclusion in JSON serialization based on PluginInfo.NoVersionFilter\\n4. Server version information exposed via the root endpoint\\n\\nThis design allows connector plugins to have different versions while maintaining API stability through a single, stable REST endpoint structure.\\n\\n## Public Health API\\n\\nThe `connect/api/` package contains the public-facing health API definitions:\\n\\n1. **ConnectorHealth.java**: Public API class providing basic health information about a connector and its tasks. Contains name, ConnectorState, Map<Integer, TaskState>, and ConnectorType.\\n\\n2. **ConnectorState.java** (Health API): Public API class for connector health state with state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\n3. **TaskState.java** (Health API): Public API class for task health state with taskId, state, workerId, and trace message fields (NO version field).\\n\\nThese health API classes differ from the REST entity classes (ConnectorStateInfo.TaskState) in that they are part of the public ConnectRestExtension API and do NOT include version fields.\\n\\n## Key Differences Between Current and Future API Versions\\n\\nThe following differences exist between the **internal REST response entities** and the **public health API**:\\n\\n**REST Response Entities** (connect/runtime/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/runtime/rest/entities/):\\n- Include a `version` field in TaskState and ConnectorState\\n- Use conditional JSON inclusion via @JsonInclude with NoVersionFilter\\n- Support filtering out undefined version values\\n\\n**Public Health API** (connect/api/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/connect/health/):\\n- NO `version` field in ConnectorState or TaskState\\n- Simpler, stable API contract\\n- Used by ConnectRestExtension implementations\\n\\n## Error Response Handling\\n\\n**REST API**: Uses unified ErrorMessage class (error_code + message)\\n**Health API**: No error response class defined (not applicable for health checks)\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":34,"oldLines":7,"newStart":34,"newLines":8,"lines":["
